Games ranked by payout for all remaining tickets

This crunches the numbers of tickets, prizes remaining, and other data for each game, and computes the payoff percentage of the tickets remaining to be sold.
For example, a Payout % of 75.00 means for each dollar you spend, there is 75 cents of prizes remaining.

Games ranked by relative number of top prizes claimed - based on percentages of all prizes vs top prize

This takes the percentage of prizes claimed for all prize levels, and compares to the percentage of prizes claimed for the top prize.
Then it is sorted by the relative difference between the top prize original published odds and the computed current 'live' odds.
Games at the top have the most improved chances of winning the top prize.
Assumption is that the prizes are spread evenly across all tickets.

Games ranked by 'weighted odds' of winning a good prize ($100,000 or more)

This computes the 'weighted odds' of winning $100,000 or more based on the number of remaining tickets in the game, the number of remaining prizes for $100,000+ prizes, as well as ticket cost.

This gives the best ticket value for winning $100,000 or more, regardless of ticket cost.

So for example, if the odds of winning $100,000 prize or more are 500, a $1 ticket weighted odds are 500. A $10 ticket has weighted odds of 5000.
